<rate>5< /rate><review>Camped at Benton Hot Springs for two nights. Due to Covid restrictions I never went into a building. Registration was outside and contactless. Specific instructions about proper campground etiquette were written down with a signed agreement and a copy for guests. Each campsite had its own tub and was as private as physically possible without constructing a complete barrier around the tubs. The campsite tubs are drained and cleaned after guests depart. <text>Camping at Benton hot springs was a worthy challenge.  Online reservations were easy, though I wish there was more info on particular sites.  Nonetheless I booked site 3 which was very relaxing, each site seemed to have its own uniqueness and privacy.  it rained/snowed on our arrival night which made things a bit cold and wet. Travel dates middle of March 2020, Chains were not required.  Light snow, ice cold temps overnight, and partly sunny days.  It was nice to arrive with tub being filled with hot water. Odorless, very hot water. (Warning for those who are sensitive to hot soaking temps) Camp site had bbq and fire pit, picnic table.  No wood to be bought on site.  Actually nothing to be bought on site so bring everything in. Otherwise a grocery store is in bishop (40 mins away) no cell signal or WiFi unless you‚Äôre staying at the ‚Äúinn‚Äù also breakfast is not included for guests staying at campsites or cabin rentals.  Bring your ez up. The best things about Benton hot springs:  Dogs allowed, Each campsite has its own private tub, & clothing optional.
For the price to camp in freezing wet temps, I would expect at least shower facilities or toilet, not Porto potties. Also some signage or information on water properties, etc. front desk staff was not very helpful.  They did not ask once how our water temp was or anything, and it was scalding at first.  Though I am pretty self sufficient I could see how guests would have a hard time navigating to their site if arriving after dark.  But the experience and hot springs makes things well worth the stay.</text><userid>117366387172873440049</userid><Response>None</Response>< username>

The Campsite at Benton Hot Springs is a piece of Heaven on Earth! The sites don't have electricity or water hookups, but come with their own private clean  HOT TUB filled with hot spring water. If you're driving from Yosemite to Las Vegas, this is an THE BEST night stop you could imagine!</Text>

Our party recently booked a stay with Benton Hot Springs and we were very excited to visit and rent the bunk house, however, our beloved Grandmother passed away within the 72 Hour cancellation notice and we had to cancel to attend her funeral.  Just be aware that this resort definitely does not 'pay it forward'  No exceptions, no refund.  We will not ever patronize them in the future because of this.  Sorry Benton you lost out on at least some future business.  Very disappointed that even the more dreaded part of the human experience isn't considered in their deliberation of 'policies'. <Date>1501011138753<//Date><user_name>Felipe Behrens< /user_name>< Review>
I stayed at the Benton hot springs last week on my cycling journey across the west from Colorado to California. The people who work here are the most caring folks in the world. when I arrived, I had a huge cut on my left leg from a collision I had had on the road during the night. I didn't have large bandages to cover the wound, but one of the ladies who works at the inn drove 38 miles to the town of Bishop where's the nearest pharmacy to get the bandages, a saline spray, neosporing, and some gummy beans for me. she went way above what was required or expected of her, and she made a huge difference for me to be able to ride the next 300 miles to San Francisco. Theresa, you are my savior and my angel! I would not have made it to the end without you. I will pay your generosity forward to someone else who is in need, and will treat them with the same care and love you showed me. Thank you!</Review>

< Text>
Family run and operated. Cozy little spot near Hermosa Beach Pier. Yes, we all know the place is small. I don't recommend it for large parties. Order to go and have a seat on the beach, it's right there. You can't beat the view. Despite the size of the place, The real magic happens in the kitchen. The art of great authentic Mexican food isn't something you just smother with cheese and salsa. It comes down to the ingredients used day in and day out. Been coming here for years and it's hard for me to decide what is my favorite meal. The main man and the master chef always has surprises up his sleeve; the best meals aren't on the menu ;)

They're extremely popular for their breakfast burritos here. Well portioned and able to create it to your liking. You can't beat the price for the amount of food you are receiving. One of my personal favorites is the bacon cheeseburger. Yes, I said the bacon cheeseburger. Get it how the chef prepares it. Overall great quality of food. The best Mexican Food in the south bay, hands down.< /Text>

< Text>
Wonderful bakery with interesting selection. Everything here is a treat. We especially love the pastries and croissants. The strawberry croissant is particularly good. The bagels are soft, chewy, and have great texture. Flavor offerings are pretty standard however: plain, blueberry, cinnamon raisin, everything, onion, poppyseed, cheese, jalapeno cheese, olive, cheese spinach, sesame, etc. I expected a place called Bageloo to offer more interesting and original bagel flavors. I also expected the bagel flavors to pack more of a punch. While the textures of the bagels were excellent, all the flavors I tried were on the light side. Again, wonderful bakery and a local Diamond Bar gem. To have this kind of quality in a small town is amazing! Lastly, do expect to pay $$ for the quality. Fifty bucks got me 12 bagels, 6 croissants, a tub of cream cheese. Yum!< /Text>

< review>
I am a big fan of Noah's Bagels in the Bay Area. I was first exposed to their food when I came here as a visitor. When I moved to the valley, one of the first places I visited was my local Noah's Bagels. They offer a bunch of bagel options, a good vegetarian veggie melt and a good veg-out bagel sandwich. My favorite is their veggie melt but with two custom changes. I request the peppercorn potato bread which has a nice spicy punch to it and I request for their best cream cheese, the jalapeno salsa. The jalapeno salsa cream cheese has a solid kick to it. Coupled with the peppercorn potato bagel, it is a killer combo, par none. Try it and you will not regret it.< /review>

<Text>No rush? No problem. The staff are friendly, and the food is decent. I tried the avocado toast and breakfast burrito my first time in, and both were acceptable for the price. The food took almost a half an hour to come with just a handful of other diners in at the time.

The avocado toast was much larger than expected, the bread was delicious and thick for being a white bread. The avocado was...bland...but a little salt, and the heart attack amount of pepper made it decent‚Äîalong with the egg. The egg itself was perfectly done, but had obviously been sitting with the rest of the food too long as it was warm‚Äînot hot.

The breakfast burrito was a decent size for the price, and had a good portion of eggs, potatoes, and cheese. Nothing special about it, but a good price point.

They have a great selection of hot sauce, including Secret Aardvark (for haba√±ero lovers).

I look forward to seeing the improvements time should bring. I‚Äôll come back to give the rest a try.

<rating>3< /rating>< Review>
Friend made a reservation here for a club banquet.

Our waiter was definitely one of the most helpful waiters. Really cared for making sure we stayed within our club budget for the reservation in ordering food and just gave wonderful service in general.

Our group split the charcuterie plate and I have to say that this is wonderful. I'm a fan of charcuterie in general and it didn't disappoint. Wonderful prosciutto and cheeses!

I personally got the oven-roasted turkey breast sandwich. It was alright. Not the best sandwich I've had, but not the worst either. I did enjoy the flavors, but the turkey was pretty dry in general. I also got the peach-infused iced tea and this was good! Not sure if they do free refills, but definitely would want to get this if I come again.

Our group also split a bunch of desserts. All time favorite is the bread pudding. The waiter recommended it and I was so glad they did. I'm not the biggest fan of bread pudding, but this one is definitely worth checking out. Not too sweet and the roaster marshmallow on top definitely adds to the flavor. The dark chocolate fudge brownie was also great -- honestly no surprises because this is such a classic dessert and it was done well. The toffee date cake was also good, but not my favorite. The strawberry marscapone cake was served in a mason jar, so not the best dish for sharing, but was definitely good as well.

Anyway, solid place for a nicer, fancier brunch, but definitely a little pricier.<//Review>

<Review>Napa Valley Grille is an outstanding fine dining establishment.

First, I was very impressed with how large it is with a nice long bar, spacious main dining area(there is also a private dining room) and a beautiful, large, airy lounge with plush couches overlooking Westwood.

I decided to enjoy my dinner in the very comfortable lounge.  My server, Carlos, did an excellent job telling me about their offerings.  I also met the Manager, Sebastian, who was very helpful and informative.  The bartender, Erik, was also very professional and on point.

Napa has a large variety of classic American cuisine to satisfy the palate.  I decided on mussels, roasted filet mignon 8 oz.(medium rare, Nebraska corn fed beef) and an Artisan cheese board.

The mussels were succulent and delicious as well as tender(many restaurants cook them too tough but these were just right).

The cheese board was wonderful.  The variety was very good with raspberries, blackberries and honey to complement the fine cheeses.

The Star was the roasted Filet Mignon.  I asked for medium rare.  The steak was cooked perfectly.  The taste in the steak juices and sauces was phenomenal.  I also added the soft cheese from the cheese board for even more flavor variety.

The Steak I had here is the best I've had in LA so far this year.  Well done Napa and Chef Carlos(also named Carlos like the server).

For wine, I had a glass of Frank, Cabernet Sauvignon 2014 Napa Valley-superb complement to the steak.

The atmosphere at Napa was very comfortable, classy and works well for either romantic dates or business meetings.

Napa Valley Grille is one of the best 10 restaurants I have been to this year in either San Diego or LA and my #1 pick for steak.< /Review><pics>None< /pics>< response>
